

         百词斩图解词典

           8482条



abase
 abase [əˈbeɪs] v.贬抑；使卑下；降低…的地位 He abased himself before her and asked her to forgive him.

abash
 abash [ə'bæʃ] v.使局促不安；使羞愧 They were quite abashed when the scary man took off all his clothes in public.

abbreviation
 abbreviation [əˌbriviˈeɪʃ(ə)n] n. 缩短;  缩写词;  省略号; He found out the true meaning of the W abbreviation on the book. 汉克在书上发现"W.W."缩写的真正含义。

abdicate
 abdicate [ˈæbdɪˌkeɪt] vi. 退位, 辞职;  vt. 辞;  放弃; King Edward the Eighth abdicated and was replaced by his brother. 爱德华八世国王退位后王位被弟弟代替了 。

abdomen
 abdomen [æbˈdoʊmən] n.腹，腹部 Eating too much can make your abdomen fat. 吃太多的话，小肚子会变胖的哟。

aberrant
 aberrant [æˈberənt] n. 离开正路的人, 反常的人;  adj. 偏离常规的;  异常的, 畸变的; John's smile was described as aberrant 约翰的微笑被说成是有点反常。

abet
 abet [əˈbet] vt. 唆使, 怂恿;  支持; It's fun to abet diet people take some desserts. 唆使正在节食的人吃甜食真是人生一大乐事。

abhor
 abhor [əbˈhɔr] v.痛恨；憎恶 Some women abhor cigarettes.

ability
 ability [əˈbɪləti] n. 能力，技能，本领 The boy has the musical ability to play the piano. 这个男孩有弹钢琴的音乐能力。

ablaze
 ablaze [əˈbleɪz] adv, adj. 着火, 燃烧;  闪耀;  激昂; The fire was soon well ablaze. 火苗很快蹿了起来。

able
 able [ˈeɪb(ə)l] adj. 能够；有能力的 Her legs don't work, but she's still able to get around. 她的腿有残疾，但是她还是能四处走动。

abnormal
 abnormal [æbˈnɒrm(ə)l] n. 畸形人;  adj. 反常的;  畸形的; It's very abnormal for a sheep to be pink! 羊是粉红色的太反常了！

aboard
 aboard [əˈbɔrd] prep. 在 (船、火车、汽车、飞机等)上, 上(船、火车、汽车、飞机等); adv. 在船(或火车、公共汽车、飞机等运输工具)上, 上船; We stayed aboard the ship for several hours. It was lovely. 我们在船上待了好几个小时，这里真爽。

abolish
 abolish [əˈbɑlɪʃ] vt. 彻底废除, 取消;  完全破坏; This president abolished slavery in America. 这位总统废除了美国奴隶制。

aboriginal
 aboriginal [ˌæbəˈrɪdʒən(ə)l] adj.土著的，原来的 n.土著居民 These aboriginal tribesmen scare the cat. 这些土著居民把汤姆吓尿了。

abortion
 abortion [əˈbɔrʃ(ə)n] n.流产；堕胎 She wants an abortion because she doesn’t want the baby. 她想堕胎因为她不想要宝宝。

abound
 abound [əˈbaʊnd] v富于；充满 Ripe grapes abounded in the sunny and fertile field. 葡萄生长在有充足阳光的肥沃土地。

above
 above [əˈbʌv] adj.上面的，上述的，上文的 adv.在上面 prep.在...上方； 过于，超出 He is flying above the cloud! 他飞上了云层！

abridge
 abridge [ə'brɪdʒ] v.删节；削减 This is the abridged version of the original, longer book. 这是之前更长的原版的删减版本。

abroad
 abroad [əˈbrɔd] prep./adv.到国外，在国外，在外 This is a picture of us when we traveled abroad. 这张照片是我们俩在国外旅行时拍摄的。

abrupt
 abrupt [əˈbrʌpt] adj.突然的；唐突的；鲁莽的 The abrupt wind blew my umbrella inside out! 突然的一阵风把我的伞都吹翻过去了。

abscond
 abscond [əbˈskɑnd] v. 逃匿，潜逃；避债 He absconded with the stolen money and was never heard from again.

absence
 absence [ˈæbsəns] n: 缺席, 外出期, 缺乏, 心不在焉; My boss noticed my co-worker's absence in the meeting. 老板注意到我同事没来开会。

absent
 absent [ˈæbsənt] prep: 缺乏;  vi: 缺席;  adj: 缺席的, 缺乏的, 心不在焉的;  vt: [absent oneself]使缺席; He is always absent, his teacher is angry about it. 樱木常常缺席，老师很生气。

absolute
 absolute [ˌæbsəˈlut] adj.完全的；绝对的；纯粹的 This room is an absolute mess. 这房间完全乱透了。

absolve
 absolve [əb'zɑlv] v.免除,解除；赦免，宽恕 I absolve you of yours sins in the name of the Father, the Son and the Holy Ghost. 我以圣父圣子的名义赦免你无罪~~~

absorb
 absorb [əbˈzɔrb] vt: 吸收, 吸引…的注意, 理解, 承受; Sponges can absorb a lot of water. 海绵可以吸收很多水分。

absorbed
 absorbed [əb'sɔːrbd] adj. 被吸引的;  被吸收的; 全神贯注的;adv. 专心致志地, 全神贯注地; n. 专心致志, 全神贯注; v. 吸收; 使全神贯注; 忍受; He was so absorbed in his book that he didn't realize the cliff. 卡卡西看书太专注了，根本没意识到他正走向悬崖.

absorption
 absorption [əbˈzɔrpʃ(ə)n] n.吸收；全神贯注；合并 I use the sponge for the absorption of liquid. 我用这个海绵来吸收液体。

abstain
 abstain [əbˈsteɪn] v.戒掉(烟\酒等)；避开；弃权 Many places will ask you to abstain from smoking. 很多场所都会要求你戒烟。

abstemious
 abstemious [əbˈstimiəs] adj. (吃喝等)有节制的，节俭的 She's rather abstemious - I can't persuade her to smoke, or to share a beer with me.

abstention
 abstention [əbˈstenʃ(ə)n] n. 戒除, 回避;  弃权;  弃权者; In an act of abstention, Steven stopped eating pizza. 为了自检，史蒂芬不再吃披萨了

abstract
 abstract [æbˈstrækt] n.摘要 adj.抽象的，深奥的 The three of them were transforming into abstract fragments. 乐乐、忧忧和冰棒正在变成抽象的碎片！

absurd
 absurd [əb'sɜːrd] n. 荒诞;  荒谬作品; adj. 荒唐的, 滑稽可笑的; It's absurd for a grown man to ride so small a bike. 成年人骑这么个小自行车是很可笑。

abundant
 abundant [əˈbʌndənt] adj.丰富的；大量的 This garden has an abundant amount of flowers. 这个花园有大量的粉色的花朵。

abuse
 abuse [əˈbjus] vt: 滥用, 虐待, 辱骂; n: 滥用, (对麻醉毒品、兴奋剂等的)非法服用, 虐待, 辱骂; Stop abusing her, you evil old lady!!! 不要再虐待她了，你这个坏嬷嬷！！！

abusive
 abusive [əˈbjusɪv] adj.辱骂的；滥用的；虐待的 The boss would become abusive to his employees when they made mistakes.

abut
 abut [əˈbʌt] v.接界，毗连；紧靠 My house abuts his, so I can hear him when he snores. 我的房子跟他的相邻，所以我可以听见他打鼾。

abyss
 abyss [əˈbɪs] n. 深渊;  深不可测的事物, 绝境;  深海;  深邃;  炼狱; The cave seemed to be an endless abyss. 这个洞穴看起来像是一个无底深渊。

academic
 academic [ˌækəˈdemɪk] adj.学术的，(综合大学中的)学院的 n.学者 They are having an academic meeting about physics. 他们正在进行物理领域的学术会议。

academy
 academy [əˈkædəmi] n. 学院 This is an academy for soldiers to train. 这是一所训练士兵的学院。

accelerate
 accelerate [əkˈseləˌreɪt] vi: 加速, 增长;  vt: 使增速, 促进; The little girl was going to fly off when the boy accelerated his skateboard. 柯南给滑板加速的时候，步美都快要飞出去了。

accelerated
 accelerated [æk'seləˌreɪtɪd] adj.加速的; The overspeed car is still in accelerated mode! 这辆超速的车还在加速的状态！

accent
 accent ['æksent] n.口音，腔调；重音；重音符号 v.重读 He has such a funny accent! 他的口音太搞笑了!

accentuate
 accentuate [ækˈsentʃuˌeɪt] v.强调；重读 Men looked at her more when she accentuated her breasts by padding her bra.

accept
 accept [əkˈsept] vi: 接受;  vt: 接受*(所提供或给予的物品), 同意, 对…信以为真, 接受, 赞同, 接纳, 容忍; I’m happy to accept your gift. 我很高兴接受你的礼物。

access
 access [ˈækˌses] n.接近；通道，入口 v. 接近 He uses his thumb to gain access to the building. 他用拇指来获得进楼许可。

accessible
 accessible [əkˈsesəb(ə)l] adj. 易使用的；可到达的；可进入的；可见到的 The bus is accessible to the disabled. 这辆公交车残疾人士亦可乘坐。

accessory
 accessory [ɪkˈsɛsəri] n. 附件, 附属物, (妇女的)装饰品;  同谋;  adj. 附属的, 辅助的;  同谋的; This part of the store contains accessories, like purses and earrings. 商店的这一部分是卖首饰的，比如项链和耳环。

accident
 accident [ˈæksɪdənt] n.事故；意外；偶然 He was badly injured in the car accident. 圣诞老公公在车祸中受伤严重。

accidental
 accidental [ˌæksɪˈdent(ə)l] adj.偶然的；非本质的 He pulls down his captain's pants---it is accidental. 樱木把队长的裤子给拉了下来---这真的纯属意外~

acclaim
 acclaim [əˈkleɪm] n. 欢呼, 赞扬, 称赞;  vi. 欢呼, 喝彩, 鼓掌欢迎;  vt. 鼓掌欢迎, 向…欢呼, 为…喝彩;  推选; Although Chinese football teams are bad, fans still acclaim for them. 虽然中国足球队是支糟糕的球队，球迷依然为他们欢呼喝彩。

acclivity
 acclivity [ə'klɪvətɪ] n.向上的陡坡 He bicycles up the acclivity.

accolade
 accolade [ˈækəˌleɪd] n. 同意，赞赏 v. 赞扬 His brilliant presentation was received with an accolade from senior management.

accommodate
 accommodate [əˈkɑməˌdeɪt] v.向…提供住处(或膳宿)；给…提供方便；容纳；使适应，顺应 The hotel room can comfortably accommodate two travelers. 这酒店的房间接纳两位旅客是没有任何问题的。

accommodating
 accommodating [əˈkɑməˌdeɪtɪŋ] adj.随和的；乐于助人的；肯通融的 v. 使适应；调节（accommodate的ing形式）；调解 The traveler thought that the hotel staff was very accommodating. 旅客觉得旅馆员工非常随和。

accommodation
 accommodation [əˌkɑməˈdeɪʃ(ə)n] n. 住宿, 住处, 舱位; 适应, 调解, 解决, 乐于助人, This hotel offers good accommodation. 这家酒店提供的住宿很好。

accompaniment
 accompaniment [əˈkʌmpənɪmənt] n.伴奏；伴随物 Ned's cup of coffee was a perfect accompaniment to the morning newspaper. 内德的咖啡是晨报的完美搭配。

accompany
 accompany [əˈkʌmpəni] v. 陪伴；为...伴奏(或伴唱) I always accompany my children to their school. 我总是陪着我的小孩们去学校。

accomplish
 accomplish [əˈkʌmplɪʃ] v. 实现；完成 Congratulations! You’ve accomplished college! 恭喜完成大学学业！

accord
 accord [əˈkɔrd] n.协议；一致；符合；(尤指国与国之间的)谅解 v.相一致；相符合；授予，赠与 Finally they all reached an accord about what the treaty should say. 他们终于就条约的内容达成了协议。

accordance
 accordance [əˈkɔrd(ə)ns] n: 符合, 授予; The little boy wore a helmet in accordance with safety regulations. 小男孩儿戴着一个头盔以符合安全规定。

accordion
 accordion [əˈkɔrdiən] n. 手风琴; adj. 可折叠的; The penguin is playing the accordion to complement their moves. 这只企鹅正在弹奏手风琴为舞蹈伴奏。

accost
 accost [ə'kɔst] v.搭讪;引诱;面对;勾引 If you want to accost me, just take one of the numbers. 如果你想搭讪我，拿个电话号码去吧  - -

account
 account [əˈkaʊnt] n.  账户，原因，估价，利益，算账 vi. 报账, 做出说明(或解释)，为…负责，受罚 vt.认为,考虑 I have no money in my bank account. 我的银行账户里没钱啦。

accountant
 accountant [əˈkaʊntənt] n.会计人员，会计师 His job is figuring out the bills as an accountant. 吕秀才这个会计的工作就是算账。

accumulate
 accumulate [əˈkjumjəˌleɪt] vt.积攒, 积累; vi.聚积; He accumulates money for future use. 他积攒了些钱以供将来使用。

accurate
 accurate [ˈækjərət] adj. 精确的, 正确的, 符合标准的; I never miss my target because my aim is so accurate. （ 矮人火枪手）我从未失手因为我瞄得很准。

accuse
 accuse [əˈkjuz] vi. 指责, 指控; vt. 指责, 控告, 把…归咎于, 使暴露; They accused each other of being wrong. 他们相互指责对方做错了。

accustom
 accustom [əˈkʌstəm] v. 使习惯于 My cat is accustomed to using the toilet, just like me! 我的猫和我一样，习惯了使用厕所。

accustomed
 accustomed [əˈkʌstəmd] adj. 习惯的, 适应了的(to); 通常的, 惯常的, 独特的; He got accustomed to the food after 10 years of living here. 住在这儿十年之后他习惯了这里的食物。

acerbic
 acerbic [əˈsɜrbɪk] adj.尖刻的； 酸涩的心情、心境或者语调 Lemons have a very strong acerbic taste, so I don't like to eat them often.

ache
 ache [eɪk] n.疼痛 v.觉得疼痛；渴望 He felt an ache  in his knee. 韦德膝盖感到一阵剧痛。

achieve
 achieve [əˈtʃiv] v. 完成，达到 I finally achieved my goal of winning the race. 我赢得了跑步比赛，终于达成了我的夙愿。

achievement
 achievement [əˈtʃivmənt] n.成绩，成就；实现，完成 Finishing college is quite an achievement. 完成本科学业是了不起的成就。

acid
 acid [ˈæsɪd] n. 【化学】酸;  酸性物质;  尖酸; adj. 酸味的;   尖刻的;  敏锐的;  含酸过多的;  酸的; Make sure not to touch the acid--it will burn. 确保不要去碰酸，它会灼伤你的。

acidic
 acidic [æˈsidik] adj.酸的，酸性的；产生酸的 Lemon juice is acidic. 柠檬水很酸。

acknowledge
 acknowledge [əkˈnɑlɪdʒ] v.承认…的权威(或主张)；对…打招呼；对…表示感谢 I'd just like to acknowledge you for your hard work: thank you! 我只是想感谢你的辛勤工作，谢谢你！

acme
 acme [ˈækmi] n.顶点，极点 The top man is the acme of the group.

acquaint
 acquaint [əˈkweɪnt] vt. 使熟悉;  使认识, 介绍; I took the chance to get acquainted with my new work colleague. 我抓住机会和我的新同事熟悉起来。

acquaintance
 acquaintance [əˈkweɪntəns] n. 认识;  了解;  熟人; We're not close friends, just acquaintances. 我们并不是亲密朋友，只是熟人而已。

acquire
 acquire [əˈkwaɪr] vt. (尤指靠自己的努力或行动或经过一个过程)获得, 学到, 取得; He wants to acquire a new empire. 他想要得到一个新的帝国。

acquisition
 acquisition [ˌækwɪˈzɪʃ(ə)n] n.掌握；获得；获得的东西 His main goal in life was the acquisition of money. 他人生的主要目标就是获得金钱。

acquisitive
 acquisitive [əˈkwɪzətɪv] adj.贪得的，物欲重的；可学到的 He was always a very acquisitive person, and devoted his life to making lots of money.

acre
 acre [ˈeɪkər] n.英亩(=6.07亩) As a farmer, I own acres and acres of land. 作为一个农民，我拥有很多亩土地。

acrimonious
 acrimonious [ˌækrɪˈmoʊniəs] adj.严厉的；辛辣的；刻薄的 We hoped to have a calm discussion, but it soon turned acrimonious.

acrobat
 acrobat [ˈækrəˌbæt] n. (表演空中飞人、走钢丝等的)杂技演员, 特技表演者, 训练有素的体操运动员;  立场观点善变, (或变化无常), 的人; The acrobat is performing how to sleep on a tight rope. 杂技演员（小龙女）正在表演如何睡在一根绷紧的绳上。

acronym
 acronym [ˈækrəˌnɪm] n.首字母缩略词 The NOW acronym stands for "no opportunity wasted." 这里的缩略词“NOW”表示的是“没有机会可以浪费”。

acrophobia
 acrophobia [ˌækrə'foʊbɪə] n. 恐高症 I shouldn't have climbed all the way up here--I have acrophobia! Ahhhhh!

across
 across [əˈkrɔs] prep.越过，在...的那边 adv.横过，在对面 She is going across the river. 她正在过河。

act
 act [ækt] n.法案；一幕 v.扮演； 举动像 He sometimes acts happy, but sometimes acts sad. 他有时表演开心，但是有时又表演悲伤。

action
 action [ˈækʃ(ə)n] n: 行动, 行为, 动作, 运转;  vt: 【法律】对…起诉; The man took action and put a gun to her head. 男子采取了行动，用枪指着她的脑袋。

activate
 activate [ˈæktɪveɪt] v.使活动起来，使开始起作用 Press the power button to activate the machine. 按下电源键开启机器（使活动起来）。

active
 active [ˈæktɪv] adj.积极的，能起作用的 An active lifestyle is important for staying healthy. 积极的生活方式对保持健康是重要的。

actively
 actively [ˈæktɪvli] adv.积极地; 活跃地; She actively asks and answers questions in class. 赫敏在课堂总是活跃提问和答问。

activity
 activity [ækˈtɪvəti] n.行动；活动；活跃 Riding a bike is also a kind of activity. 骑自行车也是一种活动。

actor
 actor [ˈæktə] n. 演员,男演员; He is a famous Kung Fu actor. 他是著名的功夫演员。

actress
 actress [ˈæktris] n.女演员 The beautiful actress loves the attention she gets from her fans. 这个漂亮的女演员很享受来自粉丝的关注。

actual
 actual [ˈæktʃuəl] adj.实际的；真实的；目前的 The actual fact is that crocodiles walk underwater instead of swimming. 事实上，鳄鱼在浅水区是靠走而不是（人们通常以为的）游泳。

actuate
 actuate [ˈæktʃuˌeɪt] v.开动(机器)；激励，驱使 Let's actuate the machine and see what happens. 让我们开动机器然后看看会发生什么。

acumen
 acumen ['ækjəmən] n.聪明，敏锐 The successful banker had a natural acumen in matters of money. 那个成功的银行家对金钱有种天生的敏锐。

acute
 acute [əˈkjut] adj: 锐利的, 敏锐的, (疼痛、妒忌等)剧烈的, 危急的, 高音的; I have a very acute, sharp pain in my stomach. 我的胃一阵剧烈地疼痛。

adage
 adage ['ædɪdʒ] n.格言, 谚语 The old adage goes like this "All shall be well, and Jack shall have Jill". But money talks, and no money no spouse. 都说“有情人终成眷属”，但票子说了才算啊~，没票子就没老婆子哎。

adamant
 adamant [ˈædəmənt] adj.强硬的，固执的 n.坚硬的东西；坚石 He was adamant about not needing any help.

adapt
 adapt [əˈdæpt] vi. 适应不同情况;  vt. 使适合;  改编; Human beings have adapted to the changing environment. 人类已经适应了不断变化的环境。

adaptation
 adaptation [ˌædæpˈteɪʃ(ə)n] n.适应，适应性的变化；改编，改写本 Gills are the physical adaptation that allows sharks to breathe underwater. 鱼鳃是为了让鲨鱼可以在水下呼吸而发生的一种身体适应性变化。

add
 add [æd] v.(to)加，增加；补充说，又说 Add some milk to the egg. 往鸡蛋里加些牛奶。

addicted

alike
 alike [əˈlaɪk] adj.相同的，相似的；相像的 The two couples are a lot alike. 这两对情侣有相当多的相似之处。（找找看~）

   avant-garde artist : n. 先锋派艺术家
  
   avant-guerre : 战前派(第二次世界大战后保持战前思想作风的人)
  
   advantaged : adj.有利的；占有利地位的；得天独厚的|动词advantage的过去式和过去分词形式.
  
   advantages : n. 优势；特点；有利；利益（advantage的复数）v. 促进（advantage的三单形式）；有利于

 congratulation [kənˌɡrætʃəˈleɪʃ(ə)n] n.(on)祝贺；祝贺词 Congratulations on your success! 祝贺你的成功！

congregate
 congregate [ˈkɑŋɡrəˌɡeɪt] v.聚集 adj.聚集在一起的 The visitors congregated around the entrance. 游客们聚集在入口处。

congress
 congress [ˈkɑŋɡrəs] n.会议，国会，议会 In America, the Congress writes laws. 在美国，由国会制定法律。

conifer
 conifer [ˈkɑnɪfər] n.针叶树；松柏科植物 Conifer trees have seed cones and needle-like leaves. 针叶树有锥形的种子和针形的叶子。

conjecture
 conjecture [kənˈdʒektʃər] n.推测；猜想 v.推测；揣摩 Eren conjectures that Levi must be Virgo. 艾伦猜测兵长一定是处女座。

conjunction
 conjunction [kənˈdʒʌŋkʃ(ə)n] n.连接；联合；连接词 In language, conjunctions are words like "and" and "but". 在语言中，连词就是像“和”和“但是”这种词。

conjure
 conjure [ˈkʌndʒər] v.变魔术，用魔法变出；想象出 And now see how I magically conjure the Ace of Hearts out of thin air!

connect
 connect [kəˈnekt] v. 连接；联想；使有联系 My phone is connected to the computer. 我的手机正连着电脑。

connection
 connection [kəˈnekʃ(ə)n] n. 连接;  连接物;  联系, 关系; This railway is an important connection between Tibet and outside. 这条铁路是西藏与外界的重要连接。

connoisseur
 connoisseur [ˌkɑnəˈsɜr] n. (艺术品等的)鉴赏家, 鉴定家, 行家; She is a wine connoisseur. She knows which wines are the best. 她是一个品酒师，她知道哪种酒是最好的。

conquer
 conquer [ˈkɑŋkər] v.征服，攻克；破除 Women conquer the world by conquering men. 女人靠征服男人来征服世界。

conquest
 conquest [ˈkɑŋˌkwest] n. 征服, 战胜;  战利品;  爱情的俘虏; The cat made a conquest of its enemy in the pillow fight. 在枕头大战中，猫咪征服了它的对手。

conscience
 conscience [ˈkɑnʃəns] n.良心，良知 I want to do something bad, but my conscience tells me not to. 我想做些坏事，但是我的良心告诉我不能做。

conscientious
 conscientious [ˌkɑnʃiˈenʃəs] adj.认真的；勤勤恳恳的 James seems like a conscientious, hard-working student. 詹姆斯看上去是一个认真努力学习的学生。

conscious
 conscious [ˈkɑnʃəs] adj. 神志清醒的；自觉的；意识到的；有意的 The patient finally became conscious after the operation. 手术过后，这位病人终于醒了。

consciousness
 consciousness [ˈkɑnʃəsnəs] n.意识，知觉；觉悟 He lost consciousness after drinking too much. 他喝得太多，失去了知觉。

consecutive
 consecutive [kənˈsekjətɪv] adj.连续的，连贯的 He rolled three consecutive sixes. 他连扔了3个6。

consensus
 consensus [kənˈsensəs] n. 一致同意, 合意; We reached a consensus in the end. 最后我们统一了意见。

consent
 consent [kənˈsent] n.同意，赞成 v.同意 I give you my consent; you can do it if you want. 我赞成你（的想法），如果你想做你就做吧。

consequence
 consequence [ˈkɑnsəkwəns] n. 结果, 后果;  结论, 推论; The consequence of eating too much is becoming fat. 吃太多的结果就是变胖。

consequent
 consequent [ˈkɑnsəkwənt] adj.作为结果(或后果)的，随之发生的 The pollution, and its consequent environmental effects, are bad for our health. 这些污染物和它们对环境造成的后果对我们的身体健康非常有害。

consequently
 consequently [ˈkɑnsəkwəntli] adv. 结果, 因此, 所以; As he has curly hair, consequently, we call him "Juanfu". 他头发很卷，所以我们叫他“卷福”。

conservation
 conservation [ˌkɑnsərˈveɪʃ(ə)n] n.保护，保存，维持 Conservation of our environment is very important. 保护环境很重要。

conservative
 conservative [kənˈsɜrvətiv] n. 保守主义者;  保守党党员;  adj. 守旧的, 保守的;   保守党的; This conservative girl refused to wear the bikini. 保守的雏田妹妹拒绝穿那件比基尼。

conservatory
 conservatory [kənˈsɜrvəˌtɔri] n.温室；音乐学校 adj.有保存力的；保存性的 We attended a concert in the conservatory.

conserve
 conserve [kənˈsɜrv] n. 蜜饯, 果酱;  vt. 保藏, 保存; 节约 She uses energy-saving bulbs to conserve energy. 她用节能灯泡来节约能源。

consider
 consider [kənˈsɪdər] v.考虑；认为 The old man is considering about his future. 这位老人正在为自己的将来做打算。

considerable
 considerable [kənˈsɪd(ə)rəb(ə)l] adj.相当大的，重要的，可观的 His strength is considerable; he exercises every day. 他的力气相当大，（因为）他每天都锻炼。

considerate
 considerate [kənˈsɪdərət] adj. 体贴的；考虑周到的 He is so considerate to look after his sick girlfriend. 他很体贴，会在女朋友生病时照顾她。

consideration
 consideration [kənˌsɪdəˈreɪʃ(ə)n] n.考虑，思考；体贴，体谅，顾及 He must take into consideration his parents and brother. 他必须把父母和弟弟都考虑进来。

consistent
 consistent [kənˈsɪstənt] adj.一致的，一贯的；连续的 All the pipes are of a consistent size. 所有的管子都是一样的尺寸。

console
 console [kən'soʊl] v.安慰，慰问 n.控制台，仪表板；落地柜 He consoles me when I feel sad about my height. 我为身高而难过的时候，瓦里斯总是安慰我。

consolidate
 consolidate [kənˈsɑlɪˌdeɪt] v.巩固，加强；把…合为一体 We consolidated three departments into one. 我们把三个部门合并成了一个。

conspicuous
 conspicuous [kənˈspɪkjuəs] adj.显著的，显而易见的 The boy looked conspicuous with his red hair along everyone else. 樱木的一头红发在茫茫众生中很显眼。

constant
 constant [ˈkɑnstənt] adj. 持续不断的;  持续的; 持久不变的, 始终如一的; n. 不变的事物;  常数, 恒量; The baby needs his mother's constant attention. 妈妈需要无时无刻都关注着宝宝。

constantly
 constantly [ˈkɒnstəntli] adv. 不断地，不变地 I am thinking about passing my exams constantly all day. 我整天心里都在（不断地）想着通过考试的事情.

constellation
 constellation [ˌkɑnstəˈleɪʃ(ə)n] n.星座，星群，一系列，一群 I showed my girlfriend many of the constellations in the sky last night. 昨晚我向女友展示了天空中的星群。

constituent
 constituent [kənˈstɪtʃuənt] adj.有选举权的；组成的 n.选民；成分 France is a constituent country of the EU. 法国是欧盟的成员国。

constitution
 constitution [ˌkɑnstɪˈtuʃ(ə)n] n. 构造;  体质;  章程;  宪法; All our country's laws must be consistent with our constitution. 我国的所有法律必须与《宪法》保持一致。

constitutional
 constitutional [ˌkɑnstɪˈtuʃ(ə)nəl] adj.宪法的；本质的；体质上的；保健的 n.保健散步；保健运动 The US has a constitutional system. 美国有一个宪法体制。

constraint
 constraint [kənˈstreɪnt] n. 限制;  强迫, 拘束; 强制 The chains serve as constraint on my mobility. 这条链子限制了我的活动能力。

constrict
 constrict [kənˈstrɪkt] v. 约束，收缩，妨碍 The rope constricts her movement. 绳子限制了她的活动。

construction
 construction [kənˈstrʌkʃ(ə)n] n. 建筑物；建造；造句 I work in construction - I build houses. 我在建筑行业工作—我盖房子。

consulate
 consulate [ˈkɑnsələt] n. 领事馆;  领事; 领事任期; 领事职位 The Chinese consulate helps Chinese citizens abroad. 中国领事馆帮助在海外的中国公民。

consult
 consult [kənˈsʌlt] v.请教，咨询；查阅；商量 She is consulting the doctor about her illness. 她正向医生咨询她的病情。

consume
 consume [kənˈsum] vt. 消耗, 耗尽;  吃光, 喝光;  毁灭; This woman bought so many expensive goods and consumed a lot of money. 纲手购物消耗了大量金钱。

consumer
 consumer [kənˈsumər] n.消费者，用户 Consumers should make healthy choices about the foods they buy. 消费者在购买食品的时候应该选择健康的食品。

consumption
 consumption [kənˈsʌmpʃ(ə)n] n. 消耗, 消费, 耗尽; Consumption of healthy food will make you feel better. 食用健康食物使你身体更好。

contact
 contact [ˈkɑnˌtækt] v. 接触；联系 n. 接触；联系 They try to contact each other by phone, but they fail. 他们试着打电话给对方，但是联系不上。(先搞懂电话怎么拿吧）

contain
 contain [kənˈteɪn] v.包含，容纳；遏制 The glass contains milk in it. 杯子里有牛奶。

container
 container [kənˈteɪnər] n. 容器；集装箱 These containers are filled with things from China. 这些集装箱里装满了从中国运来的东西。

contamination
 contamination [kənˌtæmə'neɪʃən] n. 污染；玷污；污染物 The amount of contamination in the bay is unacceptable. 海湾上污染物的数量是无法接受的。

contemplate
 contemplate [ˈkɑntəmˌpleɪt] v.沉思，对…周密考虑，注视 He sat on the floor and contemplated the case. 夏洛克盘腿坐在地上沉思着这个案子。

contemporary
 contemporary [kənˈtɛmpəˌrɛri] adj.同时代的，当代的 n.同龄人，同时代的人 The design of this kitchen is so contemporary. 厨房的设计很现代。

contemptuous
 contemptuous [kənˈtemptʃuəs] adj. 藐视的, 倨傲的; The soldiers were contemptuous towards him during the parade. 在阅兵的时候，士兵们都很藐视他。

contend
 contend [kənˈtend] v.斗争，搏斗，争论 The two fighters contend for the championship. 两个斗士在为争夺冠军而搏斗。

content
 content [kənˈtent] n. 内容, 目录;  满足;  adj.  满足的;v.  使满意 We can get ideas of a book from its content. 我们可以从一本书的目录了解它的思路。

contented
 contented [kənˈtentəd] adj.满足的；心安的 v.使…满足；使…安心 I felt very contented after I did a good job on my exam. 当我考试考好后，我感到非常的满足。

contention
 contention [kənˈtenʃ(ə)n] n. 争夺; 争论, 辩论; 论点; There were only two candidates for the job left in contention. 这个职位只剩下有两个候选人在争。

contentious
 contentious [kənˈtenʃəs] adj.好辩的，爱争论的 My sons are very contentious - when they're not arguing, they're arm wrestling.

contest
 contest [kənˈtest] n.比赛，竞争 v.争夺，争论 The contest is so fierce that we can't tell the winner now. 比赛很激烈，我们现在还看不出来谁会赢。

contiguous
 contiguous [kənˈtɪɡjuəs] adj. 相接的; 邻近的, 附近的; The two houses are contiguous; their sides are touching. 这两个房子是连着的；它们边连着边。

continent
 continent [ˈkɑntɪnənt] n. 大陆，洲 adj.克制的，禁欲的 The world has seven continents. 世界上有7大洲。

continental
 continental [ˌkɑntɪˈnent(ə)l] adj.大陆的，大陆性的 n.欧洲人 Earth was divided into seven continents by continental drift. 大陆漂移导致地球分为七个大洲。

continual
 continual [kənˈtɪnjuəl] adj.不断的，连续的；频繁的 Learning English is a long-term continual process. 学习英语是一个长期连续不断的过程。

continue
 continue [kənˈtɪnju] v.继续，连续，延伸 You can continue driving if the light is green. 如果是绿灯，你可以继续开车。

continuity
 continuity [ˌkɑntɪˈnuəti] n.连续性 Continuity means something that keeps going. 连续性是指事物持续运动。

continuous
 continuous [kənˈtɪnjuːəs] adj. 连续的;  不断的;  延长的; That genius drew a singing man with one continuous line. 那个天才用一条连续的线画了一个唱歌的人。

contort
 contort [kənˈtɔrt] v.扭曲，歪曲 The yoga master contorts her body into strange positions.

contour
 contour [ˈkɑnˌtʊr] n. 轮廓 v. 画轮廓 The contour lines join points of equal height. 等高线上的点距离地面的高度相等。

contract
 contract [ˈkɑnˌtrækt] n.合同，契约 v.订合同，收缩，缩减 We signed the contract and I bought the house. 我们签了合同后，我就买下了这栋房子。

contraction
 contraction [kənˈtrækʃ(ə)n] n.收缩，紧缩；缩写式 This diagram shows the contraction of the heart muscles. 这个图标展示了心肌的收缩过程。

contractor
 contractor [kənˈtræktər] n. 订约人; 承包人; We hired a contractor for this job. 我们为这份工作雇佣了一个承包人。

contradict
 contradict [ˌkɑntrəˈdɪkt] v.反驳；与...发生矛盾；抵触 The signs contradict with each other. which way should we go? 这些标志互相矛盾，我们应该走哪条路呢？

contradictory
 contradictory [ˌkɑntrəˈdɪktəri] n. 矛盾的事物, 矛盾因素; adj. 反驳的, 自相矛盾的; 好反驳的; These signs are contradictory - I can't obey them both. 这些标志是矛盾的，我不能同时遵守它们。

contrary
 contrary [ˈkɒntrərɪ] adj. 相反的，对立的，矛盾的 n. 相反，对立面 The lady and the man hold contrary views. 这位女士和男士持有相反意见。

contrast
 contrast ['kɑːntræst] n.对照，对比，差异 v.(with)使与...对比 In chess, the contrast between black and white is easy to see. 在国际象棋里，黑白两棋的差异显而易见。

contribute
 contribute [kən'trɪbjuːt] v.捐献，捐助，做贡献，投稿 Many people contribute money to help people in need. 很多人捐钱来帮助有需要的人们。

contribution
 contribution [ˌkɑntrɪˈbjuʃ(ə)n] n.贡献，投稿稿件，捐献物 Thank you for making a contribution to us. 感谢各位给我们的捐献。

contrite
 contrite [ˈkɑnˌtraɪt] adj.悔罪的；痛悔的 She refused to forgive him no matter how contrite he seemed.

contrive
 contrive [kənˈtraɪv] v. 设法做到；谋划，策划；设计，想出 The smart boy has contrived all kinds of inventions. 这个聪明的男孩儿已经设计出了各种各样的发明。

control
 control [kənˈtroʊl] n. 控制; 对照实验; 控制装置;  vt. 控制, 管理; The man tries to control the sound. 这个男人试着控制音量。

controversial
 controversial [ˌkɑntrəˈvɜrʃ(ə)l] adj. 引起争论的, 有争议的; The couple is discussing a controversial topic. 这对夫妇正在讨论一个争议性话题。

conundrum
 conundrum [kə'nʌndrəm] n.(答案有双关意义的)谜语；机智问答; 难题 Here comes a word-conundrum: Three birds are rapping on a tree. 出个字谜：三只小鸟在树上唱rap~ 打一字！

convene
 convene [kənˈvin] v.召集，召唤，集合 We convened at the coffee shop. 我们在咖啡店集合。

convenience
 convenience [kənˈviniəns] n. 方便 Lord Bao put the noodles on his stomach for better convenience. 为了吃起来更方便，包大人把面条放在自己的肚子上。

convenient
 convenient [kənˈviniənt] adj.方便的；便利的 Instant noodles taste horrible, but at least they're convenient. 方便面太难吃了，但是至少它们很方便。

convention
 convention [kənˈvenʃ(ə)n] n.会议；习俗；惯例 The animal officers were having a morning convention. 动物城警员们在开晨会。

conventional
 conventional [kənˈvenʃ(ə)nəl] adj.普遍的；普通的，常规的；习惯的，传统的，保守的 “Have you had your meal？”is a conventional greeting in China. “您吃了吗？”是中国普遍的打招呼的方式。

converge
 converge [kənˈvɜrdʒ] v.会聚，集中 All the paths converged on a single point. 所有的小道会合于一点。

conversant
 conversant [kənˈvɜrs(ə)nt] adj.熟悉的；精通的；亲近的 The professor is conversant with all kinds of topics. 教授很精通各种话题。

conversation
 conversation [ˌkɑnvərˈseɪʃ(ə)n] n.会话，谈话 I enjoy having conversation with friends. 我享受和朋友们的谈话。

conversely
 conversely [ˈkɑnˌvɜrsli] adv.相反地，逆地 The woman looks cool, conversely, the man looks like a pervert. 那女人看起来很酷，相反的，男人看起来像个变态。

conversion
 conversion [kənˈvɜrʒ(ə)n] n. 转变, 转换, 宗教、信仰上的转变;  【经济学】兑换; Thankfully, the conversion rate of RMB to foreign currency is getting better gradually. 感谢国家！人民币对外币的汇率逐年渐长。

convert
 convert [ˈkɑnˌvɜrt] v.使转变；使改变 This scale converts dollars to euros. 这个比例可以把美元换算成欧元。

converter
 converter [kənˈvɜrtər] n.变流器；转化器 To use your American TV in China, you need a converter. 要在中国用美国的电视，你需要一个插口转换器。

convertible
 convertible [kən'vɝtəbl] n.敞篷跑车 adj.可改变的, 自由兑换的 Convertible is designed for the man who don‘t wanna grow up？ 敞篷跑车是给不想长大的男孩设计的？

convex
 convex ['kɒnveks] n.凸面体；凸状 adj.凸出的 The convex shape of a magnifying glass makes objects appear larger. 放大镜的凸面能让物体看起来更大。

convey
 convey [kənˈveɪ] v.传送，运送；表达，传达；传播 The belt conveys the luggages out. 传送带把行李传送出来。

conveyance
 conveyance [kənˈveɪəns] n.运输；运输工具；财产让与 There are many different means of conveyance - cars, trucks, planes, and so on.

convict
 convict [kən'vɪkt] n. 犯人 v.(经审讯)证明…有罪 The convict is in prison for some pretty terrible crimes. 这个犯人因为一些很严重的罪行而入狱。

conviction
 conviction [kənˈvɪkʃ(ə)n] n. 定罪;  信服;  坚强信念; After his conviction he was handcuffed and taken off to jail. 在他被定罪以后，被戴上手铐，押进监狱。

convince
 convince [kənˈvɪns] v. 使信服，使确信
   The footprint convinces the police that the bear is the suspect. 脚印使警察确信，熊就是嫌犯。

convincing
 convincing [kənˈvɪnsɪŋ] adj. 有说服力的; 使人信服的; Michael is a very convincing speaker. 迈克说话很具有说服力。

convoluted
 convoluted [ˈkɑnvəˌlutəd] adj.旋绕的，费解的 The only path through this maze is pretty convoluted.

cook
 cook [kʊk] n. 厨师;  vi. 烹饪;  vt. 烹调, 煮, 烧; He is a great cook! 他真是个很棒的厨师！

cool
 cool [kul] adj.凉爽的，冷静的，沉着的 ；酷的 v.(使)冷却，(使)镇静 Washing hair with cold water is so cooling. 用冷水洗头特别凉爽！

coop
 coop [kup] v.把…关进笼子里；限制；拘禁 n.鸡笼；小屋；捕鱼篓 The chickens spend their day outdoors and sleep in their coop.

cooperate
 cooperate [koʊˈɑpəˌreɪt] v.协作，合作 They cooperate to defend their opponent. 樱木花道和流川枫合作防守仙道彰。

cooperation
 cooperation [koʊˌɒpəˈreɪʃ(ə)n] n.合作；协力；协作 Their cooperation will be necessary to beat this pirate in front of them. 为了赢面前的四皇凯多，基德三人的合作是必要的（还是输了）。

cooperative
 cooperative [koʊˈɑp(ə)rətɪv] adj.合作的，协作的 n.合作社 The little pigs tried to get the pizza in a cooperative way. 小猪们试着用团结协作的方式拿到比萨。

coordinate
 coordinate [koʊˈɔrdɪnət] v. 使协调，调整 n. 坐标，（一套）衣服 adj. 并列的；同等的 They coordinate all the house's colors so the colors will match well. 他们调整整个房屋的色系，使颜色更加搭配。

coordination
 coordination [koʊˌɔrdɪˈneɪʃ(ə)n] n. 同等; 协调; 调和; 对等; Synchronized swimming requires great coordination. 花样游泳需要相当高的协调性。

copper
 copper [ˈkɑpər] n.铜，铜色，铜币 Chinese ancient coins were made of copper. 中国古代钱币是铜做的。

copy
 copy [ˈkɑpi] v.抄写，复制 n.副本，拷贝 I have just learned how to copy. 我刚学会怎么复印。

copyright
 copyright [ˈkɑpiˌraɪt] n.版权，著作权 They are fighting over the copyright of that moon logo. 他们正在争夺月亮标志的版权。

coquette
 coquette [koʊˈket] n. 调情的女子 v. 不认真对待 We think she's a bit of a coquette; she's always flirting with boys.

coral
 coral [ˈkɔrəl] n. 珊瑚 There is much coral under the sea. 海底有很多珊瑚。

cord
 cord [kɔrd] n. 细绳, 索;  【电工学】电绳;  vt. 用绳、索捆扎; I can't believe that I was tripped by this cord! 我不敢相信我居然被这根细绳绊倒了！

cordless
 cordless [ˈkɔrdləs] adj. 无绳的;  (电器)不用电线的; 无线的; A cordless phone is useful if you like to do business while you're in the bath! 如果你喜欢泡澡的时候做生意的话，无线电话是很有用的。

cordon
 cordon [ˈkɔrd(ə)n] n.哨兵线，警戒线；饰带 v.布设警戒线；封锁交通 For your own safety, please do not cross the police cordon.

core
 core [kɔr] n.核心，果心，要点 My mom gives me apples with the cores cut out. 妈妈经常把切掉了苹果核的苹果给我.

cork
 cork [kɔrk] n. 软木 adj. 软木制的 v. 塞住，抑制 I popped the cork off the bottle. 我把软木塞从瓶口拔下来。

corn
 corn [kɔrn] n.玉米，(英)小麦 Sweet corn tastes best eaten with salt and butter. 甜玉米在吃的时候加上盐和黄油味道最好。

corner
 corner [ˈkɔrnər] n.角落；拐角；困境 The girl sat in the corner of the room. 女孩坐在房间的角落里。

cornerstone
 cornerstone [ˈkɔrnərˌstoʊn] n.奠基石；基础 The cornerstone of our church is a block of granite with the date of the building carved into it. 我们教堂的奠基石是一块黑色的花岗岩，上面刻有修建时间。

cornucopia
 cornucopia [ˌkɔrnjəˈkoʊpiə] n.象征丰收的羊角；装满花果及谷穗表丰饶的羊角状物；丰饶的象征 The horn contained a cornucopia of delicious fruit.

corollary
 corollary [ˈkɔrəˌleri] n.推论；必然的结果 My new result is basically just a simple corollary of Pythagoras' theorem.

coronation
 coronation [ˌkɔrəˈneɪʃ(ə)n] n.加冕，加冕礼 I'm trying on the crown before my coronation.

corporate
 corporate [ˈkɔrp(ə)rət] adj.公司的，全体的，共同的，（法人）团体的 In a corporate job, you always have to think about profit. 在公司工作，你时刻都得考虑到利益。

corporation
 corporation [ˌkɔːrpə'reɪʃn] n. 企业；社团；公司 Baicizhan is a corporation with great morals and strong work ethics!!! 百词斩是一家超有节操和职业道德的公司！！！

corps
 corps [kɔr] n. 【军事】部队;  队, 团; The army corps are ready for battle. 部队已经做好打仗的准备。

corpse
 corpse [kɔrps] n.尸体，被废弃的东西 The foul smell of death from the corpse makes him feel sick. 尸体散发的臭味让夏洛克觉得恶心。

corpulent
 corpulent ['kɔrpjələnt] adj.肥胖的 What a cute corpulent boy, he's almost as fat as me~! 好口耐的小胖墩唉，快赶上喵约翰了哟~！

correct
 correct [kəˈrekt] adj.正确的，恰当的，合适的 v.改正，纠正，矫正 His answers are all correct. 他的答案全是正确的。

correction
 correction [kəˈrekʃ(ə)n] n. 改正，修正 I used an eraser to make corrections to my homework. 我用橡皮来改正作业。

correspond
 correspond [ˌkɔrəˈspɑnd] v. 通信；符合；相当于； We correspond by email to stay in touch. 我们靠电子邮件来保持联系。

correspondent
 correspondent [ˌkɔrəˈspɑndənt] n. 通讯员, 记者; adj. 符合的, 一致的, 相当的; After the earthquake, a news correspondent was on the scene within an hour. 地震发生了以后，新闻记者在一小时之内就赶到了现场。

corresponding
 corresponding [ˌkɔːrə'spɑːndɪŋ] adj.相应的；符合的 Each medal winner should stand on the corresponding platform. 每一位奖牌得主都要站在相应的领奖台上。

corridor
 corridor [ˈkɔrɪˌdɔr] n.走廊，长条地带，回廊，通道 There is an exit at the end of the corridor. 走廊尽头有一个出口。

corrode
 corrode [kəˈroʊd] vi. 受腐蚀;  vt. 腐蚀, 侵蚀; The metal corroded because you left it out in the rain for too long. 这金属被腐蚀（生锈）了，因为它长时间被雨淋。

corrugated
 corrugated ['kɔːrəɡeɪtɪd] adj. 褶皱的 The old fence was made from corrugated iron.

corruption
 corruption [kəˈrʌpʃ(ə)n] n.腐败，贪污，堕落 That big amount of money is the evidence of corruption. 这一大堆钱就是腐败的证据。

cosmetic
 cosmetic [kɑz'mɛtɪk] n.化妆品 adj.化妆用的 Cosmetics are often used to conceal blemishes on your face. 化妆品常用来遮盖脸部色斑。

cost

costly

costume

crest

 dictionary [ˈdɪkʃəˌneri] n.词典，字典 Use this dictionary if there are any words you don't know. 如果有不认识的单词，用这本字典查查。

didactic
 didactic [daɪˈdæktɪk] adj.说教的；教诲的 If you don't mind my being didactic, let me just say - study hard!

die
 die [daɪ] v.死亡，死 Many people died in the war. 许多人在战争中死去了。

diesel
 diesel [ˈdiz(ə)l] n.内燃机，柴油机 My car has a diesel engine so it saves money. 因为我的车是柴油引擎，所以很省钱。

diet
 diet [ˈdaɪət] n. 饮食，病人或减肥者的)特种饮食 v. 节食，规定饮食 I'm trying to eat a diet of only fruits and vegetables. 我在尝试吃只有蔬菜水果的节食餐。

dietary
 dietary [ˈdaɪəˌteri] adj.饮食的，与饮食有关的 Your dietary needs can be satisfied by fruit. 你的饮食可以用水果满足。

differ
 differ [ˈdɪfər] v.差异；不同 His skin color differs from the others'. 他的肤色和别人的都不一样。

difference
 difference [ˈdɪf(ə)rəns] n.差别 Can you find the differences between these two pictures? 你能找出两幅图的不同吗？

different
 different [ˈdɪf(ə)rənt] adj. 不同的，有差异的 The red thing was a different color. 红色那个颜色不同。

differentiate
 differentiate [ˌdɪfəˈrenʃiˌeɪt] v.使有差异；区别 It's easy to differentiate between the orange and purple flowers. 很容易区分橙色和紫色的花。

difficult
 difficult [ˈdɪfɪkəlt] adj. 困难的, 难做的;  难解的;  难对付的, 不易相处的; This game is difficult for the man. 这个游戏对他而言很难完成。

difficulty
 difficulty [ˈdɪfɪkəlti] n. 困难;  难事, 难点;  经济拮据;  分歧;  麻烦; Riding up the hill is really a big difficulty. 骑车上山真是一大难事。

dig
 dig [dɪɡ] n. 掘，挖 v. 掘，挖 To install the swimming pool they used a machine to dig a big hole. 为了修一个游泳池，他们用机器挖一个大洞。

digest
 digest [daɪ'dʒest] v.消化 n.摘要 The food he ate was hard to digest. 他吃的食物很难消化。

digestion
 digestion [daɪˈdʒestʃ(ə)n] n.消化；消化能力；领悟 Good digestion keeps your body healthy. 好的消化力能保持你的身体健康。

digital
 digital [ˈdɪdʒɪt(ə)l] adj. 数字的，计数的 A digital stopwatch is very precise. 电子秒表很精确。

dignity
 dignity ['dɪɡnəti] n.威严，威风；端庄；尊严，高贵 The policeman and the firefighter serve with dignity and honor. 警察和消防队员怀着尊严和荣誉任职。

digress
 digress [daɪˈɡres] v.离题；走向岔道 Don't digress - get back to the point!

dike
 dike [daɪk] n.堤防，堤坝；障碍物；（英）壕沟 v.筑堤防护；开沟排水 The terraced rice fields are walled off by low earth dikes.

dilapidated
 dilapidated [dɪˈlæpɪˌdeɪtəd] adj. 倾坍的;  破旧的, 破烂的; This house is dilapidated!--I couldn't possibly live here. 这房子各种破旧衰败——我才不可能住在这里呢。

dilate
 dilate [daɪˈleɪt] v. 使膨胀，扩张，膨胀 My pupil dilated when you turned off the light. 当你关灯的时候我的瞳孔将扩大。

dilemma
 dilemma [dɪ'lemə] n.困境，左右为难
   He is in dilemma between the two desserts. 银时在两份甜点中左右为难。

diligent
 diligent [ˈdɪlɪdʒənt] adj.勤奋的，用功的 He is a diligent ninja at studying. 鹿丸是个勤奋学习的忍者。

dilution
 dilution [daɪ'ljuːʃn] n.稀释；稀释法；冲淡物 The dilution of the red coloring turned the water pink. 红色被稀释后，将水染成了粉红色。

dim
 dim [dɪm] v. 变暗淡 adj. 暗淡的，弱的 The light is very dim. I can't see clearly. 光线十分昏暗，我看不清。

dime
 dime [daɪm] n. (美国、加拿大的)10分硬币;  一角硬币; I want a lollipop, daddy. It only costs a dime. 我想要买棒棒糖，爸。只花一毛钱而已。

dimension
 dimension [daɪ'menʃn] n.尺寸，尺度；面积，维度 These shapes have three dimensions. 这些图形有三个维度。

dimensional
 dimensional [dɪ'menʃənəl] adj.空间的，维度的 When I add shading to the drawing it makes it look three dimensional. 我给画加上阴影之后，它看起来很立体。

diminish
 diminish [dɪˈmɪnɪʃ] v.变小，降低，减少 This is terrible! Our profits are still diminishing - why? 这太糟糕了！我们的利润还在减少，为什么呢？

dimly
 dimly [ˈdɪmli] adv.朦胧地；微暗 The room was dimly lit with two small candles. 那个房间只有两个小蜡烛，很黑暗。

din
 din [dɪn] n.喧闹声，嘈杂声 v.喧闹，喋喋不休地说 I had to shut my ears because the din was so loud. 嘈杂声太大了，我不得不捂住耳朵。

dine
 dine [daɪn] v. 吃饭；进餐 Let's dine together tonight. 今晚一起吃饭吧。

dining
 dining ['daɪnɪŋ] n.吃饭，进餐 Dining with the family is important. 一家人共进晚餐是重要的。

dinosaur
 dinosaur [ˈdaɪnəˌsɔr] n. 恐龙 They made friends with this dinosaur. 大雄他们和这只恐龙变成了朋友。

dip
 dip [dɪp] v.浸，蘸 n.倾斜，下降；浸渍 The bird dips its feet into the water. 这只鸟把它的脚浸入水中。

diploma
 diploma [dɪ'ploʊmə] n. 毕业文凭;  奖状; vt. 发给…毕业文凭; After four years of hard work, I finally got my college diploma. 经过四年的辛勤努力，我终于拿到了大学毕业证。

diplomatic
 diplomatic [ˌdɪpləˈmætɪk] adj.外交的，从事外交的，老练的，圆滑的 They put on diplomatic faces, although on the inside they're angry. 虽然内心都很愤怒，表面上他们还是一副圆滑的表情。

dire
 dire [daɪr] adj. 可怕的；悲惨的；极端的 These meteors will have dire consequences for life on Earth.

direct
 direct [də'rekt] adj. 直达的; 笔直的;  直接的;  率直的; vi. 指导;  引路, 当向导;  导演;  领唱; vt. 指导, 引导;  管理;  导演; adv. 直接地, 径直地; The direct flight on the map saves more time. 地图上的直飞航线更节省时间。

direction
 direction [də'rekʃn] n.方向，方位；指令，说明 The road goes in many directions. 道路四通八达。

director
 director [də'rektər] n.指导者，主任，导演 The man is the director of this department. 弗瑞是神盾局的局长。

directory
 directory [də'rektəri] n.人名地址录，(电话)号码簿 adj. 指导的；咨询的 Just look up his telephone number in the directory. 快去号码簿里找他的电话号码。

dirge
 dirge [dɜrdʒ] n.挽歌；哀悼歌 I'm listening to a very sad dirge; it's very unhappy music.

dirt
 dirt [dɜː(r)t] n.尘，土，污物，污垢 I want to wash the dirt from my hands. 手上沾满了泥。

dirty
 dirty [ˈdɜrti] adj.弄脏的，下流的 v.弄脏，玷污 adv.不公平地，不诚实地 My hands are dirty. I must wash them. 我的手很脏，必须得洗了。

disability
 disability [ˌdɪsəˈbɪləti] n.残疾；无能；无资格；不利条件 Although the boy has a disability, he likes painting. 尽管这个男孩残疾，但他喜欢画画。

disable
 disable [dɪsˈeɪb(ə)l] vt. 使无能, 使伤残, 使丧失活动能力;  使在法律上不能; They are both disabled after falling from a high tower. 从高塔上跳下来之后，他们俩都残废了。

disadvantage
 disadvantage [ˌdɪsədˈvæntɪdʒ] n.不利，不利地位，弱点；弊端 Due to his disadvantage in height, he drowned in the river. 由于身高上的劣势，力丸在河道被淹死了。

disagree
 disagree [ˌdɪsəˈɡri] v.意见不同，不一致 The boy disagrees with his mother. 这个男孩与妈妈意见不一致。

disagreement
 disagreement [ˌdɪsəˈɡrimənt] n.分歧；意见不合；争执，争论；不同，差异 The disagreement between them always causes them to fight. 他们总是因为着装上的分歧而打架。

disappear
 disappear [dɪsəˈpɪə(r)] v.消失；失踪 He made a bird disappear！ 他让一只鸟消失了！

disappearance
 disappearance [ˌdɪsəˈpɪrəns] n.不见，消失 The parents are surprised at the disappearance of their child! 父母对孩子的失踪感到震惊!

disappoint
 disappoint [ˌdɪsəˈpɔɪnt] v.使失望，使扫兴，使受挫折 The fact that she doesn't like him disappointed him. 小樱不喜欢他，这件事让鸣人很挫败。

disappointed
 disappointed [ˌdɪsəˈpɔɪntəd] adj.失望的 He was disappointed that his favorite football team lost. 他很失望，因为他最喜欢的足球队输了。

disappointment
 disappointment [ˌdɪsəˈpɔɪntmənt] n.失望；沮丧 His disappointment at not getting the job showed in his face. 他未得到工作，沮丧就写在脸上。

disapprove
 disapprove [ˌdɪsəˈpruv] vi. 不赞成; vt. 不同意, 不赞成*; Dad's thumbs down shows that he disapproves my idea to get a tattoo. 老爸大拇指向下表示他不赞成我去纹身。

disarm
 disarm [dɪsˈɑrm] v.使人消除敌意；放下武器 She was learning how to use martial arts to disarm a criminal with a knife. 她在学习如何用武术让带着刀的罪犯放下武器。

disarray
 disarray [ˌdɪsəˈreɪ] n.混乱，漫无秩序 Your room is in total disarray! Clean it up now! 你的房间简直杂乱无章！现在就打整它！

disaster
 disaster [dɪˈzæstər] n.灾难，天灾 The whole city is destroyed. It’s a real disaster. 整座城市都被毁了，真是一场灾难。

disastrous
 disastrous [dɪˈzæstrəs] adj.灾难性的 Two people died in a disastrous mishap. 两人死于这场惨烈的事故。

disc
 disc [dɪsk] n.磁盘，圆盘，椎间盘 The music is stored in the disc. 音乐储存在这张唱片里。

discard
 discard [dɪsˈkɑrd] v.丢弃，抛弃，遗弃 He discarded his suit because he no longer wanted to be a hero. 蜘蛛侠丢弃了他的套装，因为他不想再当英雄了。

discharge
 discharge [dɪsˈtʃɑrdʒ] n. 发射;   解雇;   放电;  v  发射;  放电;  解雇；排出 The ass-itch boy spoiled the circuit and discharged the electricity. 熊孩子破环电路，把电放了。

disciple
 disciple [dɪˈsaɪp(ə)l] n. 信徒, 门徒;  耶稣的信徒(或门徒、使徒); This is a famous painting of Jesus' last supper with his disciples. 这是一幅著名的画作叫做《耶稣和门徒最后的晚餐》。

disciplinary
 disciplinary [ˌdɪsəˈplɪnəri] adj. 纪律的, 纪律严明的;  训练的;  学科的; Saluting you superiors is a disciplinary act. 向上级领导敬礼是纪律严明的表现。

discipline
 discipline [ˈdɪsəplɪn] n. 纪律；学科；训练 v. 训练 The discipline of the Red Army is very strict. 红军的纪律十分严格。

disclose
 disclose [dɪsˈkloʊz] v. 透露，泄露 When the man disclosed his wrongdoings to his wife, she was very angry. 当这个男人向他老婆坦白他做的错事以后，他老婆非常生气。

discombobulate
 discombobulate [ˌdɪskəm'bɒbjəˌleɪt] vt. 使混乱, 使困惑, 挫败; All these questions I can't answer just discombobulate me. 这些我答不上来的问题让我很泄气。

disconcert
 disconcert [ˌdɪskənˈsɜrt] v.使仓皇失措；使困惑；破坏 I was disconcerted to realize that the whole idea behind my Master's Thesis was wrong.

disconnect
 disconnect [ˌdɪskəˈnekt] v. 拆开，使分离 The phone company disconnected my phone service because I didn't pay my bills. 电话公司切断了对我的服务，因为我没有付我的账单。

disconsolate
 disconsolate [dɪsˈkɑnsələt] adj.郁郁不乐的，孤独的，前途黯淡的 He was disconsolate - his girlfriend had dumped him.

discontent
 discontent [ˌdɪskənˈtent] n. 不满 adj. 不满的 Why the discontent? Your hair looks fine. 有什么不满？你的头发看上去挺好的。

discord
 discord [ˈdɪsˌkɔrd] n.不和，争吵；(声音)不和谐 Discord between this couple has lasted for years. 哎，毛利夫妇不和多年。

discount
 discount [dɪsˈkaʊnt] v. 不信，把…打折扣，怀疑地看待 n. (价格、债款等)折扣 Pizza Hut offers discounts for college students with valid student IDs. 必胜客会给带有效学生证的大学生顾客们打折哦。

discourage
 discourage [dɪs'kɜːrɪdʒ] v.使泄气，使失去信心；阻止； This girl's words discourage him. 这个女生的话让他很泄气。

discourse
 discourse [ˈdɪsˌkɔrs] n.演讲，论述，讲道，交谈 v.演讲，谈论 They are having a discourse about the general world situation. 刘备和诸葛亮正在谈论天下大势。

discover
 discover [dɪˈskʌvər] v.发现，找到，发掘，揭露 I hope to discover a cure for AIDS. 我希望能找到艾滋病的治疗办法。

discovery
 discovery [dɪˈskʌvəri] n.发现；被发现的事物 Their discovery of treasure really excites them. 发现宝藏让他们激动万分。

discreet
 discreet [dɪˈskrit] adj.谨慎的，思虑两全的 Please be discreet about this; Do not tell anybody. 请你对这件事保持慎重，不要告诉给任何人。

discrepancy
 discrepancy [dɪˈskrepənsi] n.不一致，差异，不符 There's quite a discrepancy between the two; they're not the same at all. 它们之间差异很大，它们根本就不是同一个。

discrimination
 discrimination [dɪˌskrɪmɪˈneɪʃ(ə)n] n.歧视，偏见 There could also be discrimination between the brothers. 兄弟之间也会存在歧视呢~

discuss
 discuss [dɪˈskʌs] v.讨论；论述 The students discussed the topic on the blackboard. 学生们讨论了黑板上的话题。

discussion
 discussion [dɪˈskʌʃ(ə)n] n.讨论，谈论；论述 The team is having a discussion. 这个团队正在讨论问题。

disdain
 disdain [dɪsˈdeɪn] n. 蔑视, 鄙视; vt. 鄙视;  不屑; He disdained his rival's contribution. 樱木很鄙视竞争对手(流川枫)做出的贡献。

disease
 disease [dɪˈziz] n.疾病 The man has a heart disease. Get him to the hospital! 那个男人有心脏病,快送他去医院！

disembark
 disembark [ˌdɪsɪmˈbɑrk] vi. 上岸, 登陆, 下车, 下飞机;  vt. 使上岸;  使登陆; We disembarked from the helicopter at the top of the mountain. 在山顶，我们从直升飞机上下来。

disengage
 disengage [ˌdɪsɪnˈɡeɪdʒ] v. 分开 I'm trying to disengage these two rings from each other.

 disgorge [dɪsˈɡɔrdʒ] v.呕出；（水）流走 After drinking too much, the woman went to the bathroom to disgorge the contents of her stomach.

disgrace
 disgrace [dɪsˈɡreɪs] n. 耻辱;  不光彩;  失宠;  vt. 使丢脸, 给…带来耻辱;  使失宠; He disgraces me by forcing me to crawl between his legs. 我受到了胯下之辱。

disguise
 disguise [dɪsˈɡaɪz] n. 伪装物;  伪装;  托辞;  伪装的方式;  vt. 假扮;  伪装;  掩饰; Miss Bear disguises herself as a panda by wearing black stockings. 熊小姐通过穿黑丝袜把自己伪装成了一个熊猫。

disgust
 disgust [dɪsˈɡʌst] n.恶心 v.使作呕，使厌恶
   What really disgusts me isn't one, but a half worm in an apple. 真正让我恶心的不是在苹果发现一条虫而是半条。

disgusting
 disgusting [dɪsˈɡʌstɪŋ] adj. 令人厌恶的;  令人无法接受的; Take a shower! You smell disgusting! 快去洗澡，你闻起来真恶心！

dish
 dish [dɪʃ] n.碟，盘子；菜肴 We have a big dish for our dinner. 我们的晚餐有个好菜。

disheveled

dishonor
 dishonor [dɪsˈɑnər] n.不光彩，不名誉 v.使丢脸；凌辱 He brought dishonor to himself by making a big mistake at work. 他工作时的失误给他自己蒙了羞。

disillusion
 disillusion [ˌdɪsɪˈluʒ(ə)n] n. 醒悟; 幻灭;  vt. 使醒悟;  使不抱幻想;  给…泼冷水; Due to my girlfriend's unfaithful behavior, my hope was replaced by disillusion. 由于女友的不忠行为，我的期望彻底毁灭了。

disinfect

disintegrate
 disintegrate [dɪsˈɪntɪˌɡreɪt] vi. 碎裂;  瓦解;  衰变;  vt. 使碎裂, 使分裂;  使衰变; The abandoned buildings are already starting to disintegrate. 废弃的大楼已经开始碎裂了。

disinter
 disinter [ˌdɪsɪnˈtɜr] v.掘出；发掘；显露 The courts ordered us to disinter the body from the ground.

 disinterested [dɪsˈɪntrəstəd] adj.无私的；公正的；冷漠的；廉洁的 The judge maintained a disinterested attitude, favoring neither the plaintiff nor the defendant. 法官持公正的态度,既不偏向原告也不偏向被告。

disk
 disk [dɪsk] n.圆盘，唱片；磁盘 I'll put the music on a compact disk. 我会把音乐放到一张压缩磁盘上。

dislike
 dislike [dɪsˈlaɪk] v.不喜欢，厌恶 n.不喜欢，厌恶 He dislikes that hat, although it really suits him. 索隆并不喜欢那顶帽子，尽管那很适合他。

dislodge
 dislodge [dɪsˈlɑdʒ] v.驱逐；移去；取出 He almost made the jump, but dislodged the bar.

dismal
 dismal [ˈdɪzməl] n. 低落的情绪;  adj. 惨淡的; 沉闷的, 凄凉的; The dismal weather indicates that the rain is coming soon. 阴沉的天气预示着要下雨了。

dismantle
 dismantle [dɪsˈmænt(ə)l] v.拆开；拆除 The building needed to be dismantled to make room for new ones.

dismay
 dismay [dɪsˈmeɪ] n.沮丧，失望，气馁 v.使惊恐，使失望，使气馁 The crazy woman cried out in dismay. 这个疯狂的女人在沮丧中放声大喊。

dismember
 dismember [dɪsˈmembər] v.肢解；瓜分 Don't dismember your doll unless you can put it back together again! 除非你能将它拼装好，否则不要拆开你的玩偶。

dismiss
 dismiss [dɪsˈmɪs] v.不再考虑；解雇 The coach was dismissed by the club. 穆里尼奥被切尔西炒了。

disobey
 disobey [ˌdɪsəˈbeɪ] v. 违反；不服从 You're such a tiny dog - how dare you disobey me? 你这么一只小狗怎么还敢不服从我？

disorder

 image [ˈɪmɪdʒ] n. 图像，形象，映像 This X-ray image shows me you need to take more care of your teeth. 这张X光片告诉我，你需要多多照顾你的牙齿。

imaginary
 imaginary [ɪˈmædʒɪˌneri] adj.想象中的，假想的 In my imaginary world, I am a princess who lives in a big castle. 在我的幻想世界里，我是一个住在大城堡里的公主。

immigrant
 immigrant [ˈɪmɪɡrənt] n.移民 The immigrants have left their home country to start a new life. 移民者离开他们原来的国家，开始了一段崭新的生活。

 institution [ˌɪnstɪˈtuʃ(ə)n] n. 机构；创立；制度；习俗 The United Nations is an international institution. 联合国是一家国际机构。

instruction
 instruction [ɪnˈstrʌkʃ(ə)n] n. 教学；指示；指导 The little girl is giving instructions to the two boys. 比司吉·酷露佳在指导小杰和奇犽。

instructor
 instructor [ɪnˈstrʌktər] n.指导者，教员.教练 Our instructor gave us a lesson everyday. 指导员每天都会给我们上课。

instrument
 instrument [ˈɪnstrəmənt] n.仪器，工具，乐器 i can play all of these musical instruments. 我会玩下列所有的乐器。

instrumentalist
 instrumentalist [ˌɪnstrəˈment(ə)lɪst] n.乐器演奏家； 工具主义者 My cousin is an instrumentalist in the New York Symphony orchestra. 我的表妹是纽约交响乐团的一个乐器演奏家。

insufficient
 insufficient [ˌɪnsəˈfɪʃ(ə)nt] adj.不足的
   One pea?! This meal is totally insufficient. 只有一个豌豆？这顿饭完全不够吃。

insulate
 insulate [ˈɪnsjəˌleɪt] v. 隔离，使隔绝(以免受到影响)；使绝缘；使隔热；使隔音 This mug insulates my coffee, keeping it hot. 这个马克杯能隔热，保温我的咖啡。

insulation
 insulation [ˌɪnsjəˈleɪʃ(ə)n] n. 隔离;  绝缘; These wires are made of copper, with colored plastic insulation. 这些线是铜质的，由彩色的绝缘塑料包裹。

insulin
 insulin [ˈɪnsəlɪn] n.胰岛素 I need insulin injections to help my body process sugar. 我需要注射胰岛素来帮助我的身体消化糖分。

insult
 insult [ɪnˈsʌlt] v.侮辱，凌辱 n.侮辱的言词或行为 It doesn't help to insult other drivers. 辱骂其他的司机也无济于事。

insurance
 insurance [ɪnˈʃʊrəns] n.保险，保险费，保险业 I bought insurance for my car. 我给我的车上了保险。

insure
 insure [ɪnˈʃʊr] v.保险，给…保险；保证 I insure my car against accident and theft. 我为我的车上了事故险和偷盗险。

insurmountable
 insurmountable [ˌɪnsərˈmaʊntəb(ə)l] adj. 不能克服的，不能超越的，难以对付的 The castle's defenses were virtually insurmountable. 那个城堡的防御实际上是不可攻破的。

insurrection
 insurrection [ˌɪnsəˈrekʃ(ə)n] n.造反，叛乱 The rebels started an insurrection against the King. 叛逆分子们制造了反抗国王的暴动。

intact
 intact [ɪnˈtækt] adj. 未受损的, 完整无缺的; The glass remained intact after it was dropped. 这个杯子掉下来竟然还是完好无缺。

intangible
 intangible [ɪnˈtændʒəb(ə)l] adj.不可捉摸的，无形的 I reached out to touch the spectral hand, but it was intangible, like a ghost's. 我伸出手去触摸幽灵般的手，但是它却无法触及，就像鬼一样。

integer
 integer [ˈɪntədʒər] n.整数；整体 When it comes to ranking, one is the only integer I like to see. 涉及到排名时，1就是我唯一想看到的整数。

integrate
 integrate [ˈɪntɪˌɡreɪt] v.(into,with)(使)成为一体,(使)结合,(使)合并 Two have been integrated into one and that means love. 它们合体了，沐浴在满满的爱之中。

integrity
 integrity [ɪnˈteɡrəti] n. 正直, 真诚;  廉正;  完整;  完善; Lord Bao was well known for his integrity in China. 包大人在中国以其正直而家喻户晓。

intellectual

intelligent
 intelligent [ɪnˈtelɪdʒənt] adj. 聪明的 It's hard to measure my IQ as I'm so intelligent. 要测试我的IQ是很难的，因为姐如此机智。

 intend [ɪnˈtend] v.想要，打算，企图 Hi, cat, what do you intend to do - eat me, or just watch me? 嗨，小猫，你想干吗？吃掉我还是只是看着我。

intense

intensity

intensive
 intensive [ɪnˈtensɪv] adj.加强的，强调的，精耕细作的 She became stronger after intensive physical training. 经过强化身体训练后，她变得更加强壮了。

interested
 interested ['ɪntrəstɪd] adj.感兴趣的；有成见的；有权益的 They were all interested in class. 他们都对课程很感兴趣。

interesting

interior

 potential [pəˈtenʃ(ə)l] adj.潜在的 n.潜力 He has a lot of potential--I could see him going places. 他很有潜力,我能看见他在上位。

potion
 potion [ˈpoʊʃ(ə)n] n.一剂，一服；毒药，魔药 He held a potion which could grant his wish. 哈利举着一瓶能满足他愿望的魔药。

potted
 potted [ˈpɑtəd] adj.盆栽的；罐装的 A potted plant is a nice gift for someone who has a new home. 一个盆栽植物是送给刚搬新家的朋友的好礼物。

potter
 potter [ˈpɑtər] n. 陶工 The potter made a bowl out of clay. 制陶人用黏土做了一个碗。

pottery
 pottery [ˈpɑtəri] n. 陶器；陶艺；陶艺厂 Pottery is one of my favorite hobbies. 陶艺是我的爱好之一。

poultry
 poultry [ˈpoʊltri] n.家禽肉，家禽 Poultry, like pork and chicken, is my favorite kind of food. 家禽，例如猪肉和鸡肉，是我最喜欢吃的食物。

pounce
 pounce [paʊns] n. 猛扑, 飞扑;  vi. 猛扑, 突然袭击;  vt. 扑过去抓住; The predator pounced the little creature from the bush. 狮子狗从草丛扑向了提莫。

pound
 pound [paʊnd] n.英镑，磅 v.(连续)猛击，捣碎 I have 60 pounds in total. 我总共有60英镑。

pour
 pour [pɔr] v.倒入，注入；下（雨） I poured a glass of milk. 我倒了一杯牛奶。

pout
 pout [paʊt] n.撅嘴，板脸，生气 v.撅嘴，绷脸 Don't pout--why don't you come play with us?

poverty
 poverty [ˈpɑvərti] n. 贫困，贫穷 He has lived in poverty since he joined the beggar gang. 自从加入丐帮后，他就过着穷困潦倒的生活。

powder
 powder [ˈpaʊdər] n. 粉；火药 v.抹粉 People, stay away from the powder！ 离松本身边的粉末（灰猫始解）远一点！

power
 power [ˈpaʊər] n.能力，权力，电源，幂 v.驱动；提供动力 His arms have a lot of power. 他的手臂很有力。

powerful
 powerful [ˈpaʊrf(ə)l] adj.强有力的；有权威的 He has two powerful arms. 他有两只强有力的手臂。

practical
 practical [ˈpræktɪk(ə)l] adj. 实用的；实际的；实践的 This robot is so practical; it can even cook. 这机器人还能做饭，简直太实用了。

practice
 practice [ˈpræktɪs] v. 经常作；实践 n. 练习；实行 You should practice playing the piano every day. 你应该每天练习钢琴。

pragmatic
 pragmatic [præɡˈmætɪk] adj.国事的，团体事务的；实际的，注重实效的 He is a very pragmatic man, always focusing on what specifically to do next. 他是个很注重实效的人，永远都专注在每件接下来要完成的事情上。

prairie
 prairie ['preri] n. 大草原, (尤指) 北美大草原;  草原地带; Many cows eat grass on the prairie. 许多奶牛在大草原上吃草。

prate
 prate [preɪt] v.大谈特谈，唠叨 These two love to prate on about their hairdos and important stuff like that.

prattle
 prattle [ˈpræt(ə)l] v.闲聊；胡说；小孩般说话 n.无聊话；咿咿呀呀声 The women love to drink coffee and prattle to each other.

pray
 pray [preɪ] v.祈祷，祈求，请求，恳求， The woman closed her eyes and began to pray. 那个女人闭上眼睛开始祈祷。

prayer
 prayer [prer] n.祈祷，祷告，祷文 In some families they say a prayer together before each meal. 在一些家庭中他们会在进餐前一起祷告。

preach
 preach [pritʃ] v.传教，讲道，鼓吹 The monk preaches about religion to us; I wish he'd shut up. 这个修道士一直向我们鼓吹宗教，我希望他能闭嘴。

precarious
 precarious [prɪˈkeriəs] adj. 不稳定的;  危险的;  可疑的;  说不定的; The bridge was very precarious; we could have fallen off at any time. 该桥非常危险，我们随时有可能掉下去。

precaution
 precaution [prɪˈkɔʃ(ə)n] n.预防措施，警惕，戒备 We wear masks as a precaution against catching a cold. 我们戴口罩来预防感冒。

preceding
 preceding [prɪˈsidɪŋ] adj.在前的，在先的 The preceding day was Sunday, so this must be Monday. 因为前一天是周日，所以今天是周一。

precious
 precious [ˈpreʃəs] adj.珍贵的，宝贵的 Precious gems like diamonds are very valuable. 像钻石一样珍贵的宝石是很贵重的。

precipice
 precipice [ˈpresəpɪs] n. 悬崖;  危险的处境, 灾难的边缘, 濒危点; Be careful at the precipice--you might fall off. 在悬崖边得小心——你有可能摔下去。

precipitation

precipitous
 precipitous [prɪˈsɪpɪtəs] adj.险峻的；急躁的，鲁莽的 I felt at peace standing on the precipitous cliff overlooking the magnificent landscape. 我站在险峻的悬崖边上俯瞰广袤的大地时感到很平静。

precise
 precise [prɪˈsaɪs] adj. 精确的，恰好的 This instrument gives precise measurements. 这只仪器显示出精确的测量结果。

precision
 precision [prɪˈsɪʒ(ə)n] n.精确，精密度 This is a high precision tool for measurements. 这个仪器用来精密测量。

preclude

precocious

predict
 predict [prɪˈdɪkt] v.预言，预告，预测 The man predicted that the woman will have a baby girl. 他预言这位妇女会生一个女孩。

predisposition
 predisposition [ˌpridɪspəˈzɪʃ(ə)n] n.倾向；素质；易染病体质 Redheads often have a hereditary predisposition to skin disease. 红发常伴随遗传性皮肤病体质。

predominant
 predominant [prɪˈdɑmɪnənt] adj.占主导地位的，显著的，占优势的 The white pieces were predominant on the chess board, so I lost the game. 棋盘上白色棋子占上风（主导地位），所以我输掉了比赛。

preempt
 preempt [priˈempt] v.制止，以先买权取得，取代 I preempt the dominoes' falling by stopping them with my hand.

prefer

preferable
 preferable [ˈpref(ə)rəb(ə)l] adj.(to)更可取的，更好的 My last job was okay, but this job is preferable. 我上一个工作还好，但这个工作更棒。

preference
 preference [ˈpref(ə)rəns] n.偏爱，优先，优先权 I have a preference for fruit. 我对水果有偏爱。

pregnant
 pregnant [ˈpreɡnənt] adj.怀孕的，充满的 She was happy because she finally got pregnant. 苏菲很高兴她终于怀上孩子了。

prehistoric

 prodigious [prəˈdɪdʒəs] adj.异常的，奇妙的；巨大的 This forest is full of prodigious trees 这片森林长满了高大的树木。

prodigy
 prodigy [ˈprɑdədʒi] n. 奇事; 天才; 壮举; Our three-year-old son is a piano prodigy - he's already playing Mozart. 我们3岁的孩子是个钢琴天才 - 他已经能够弹奏莫扎特的曲子了。

produce
 produce [prəˈdus] n. 农产品;  vi. 生产; 产生; 创作;  vt. 生产; 创作; 产生; The factory produced things quickly. 工厂生产产品速度很快。

product
 product [ˈprɑdəkt] n.产品，产物；(乘)积 These products are made of milk. 这些产品都是由牛奶制成的。

production
 production [prə'dʌkʃn] n.生产，产量，生产过程；上演的戏 Car production is very common in China. 汽车生产在中国很普遍。

productive
 productive [prəˈdʌktɪv] adj.多产的；富有成效的 He had a productive day, cleaning most of the weeds out of his garden. 他清除了花园里大多数的杂草，度过了颇有成效的一天。

profess
 profess [prəˈfes] v. 表示，承认；宣称信仰 He got down on his knee and professed his love to her. 吕秀才单膝下跪，向郭芙蓉示爱。

profession
 profession [prəˈfeʃ(ə)n] n. 职业; 同行; 声明; 立誓信教; These are three of the eight professions that can be selected. 剑灵中一共有8个职业可以选择，而这3个只是其中的一部分。

professional
 professional [prəˈfeʃ(ə)nəl] adj. 职业的 n. 专业人员 My parents want me to have a professional career  - but which profession should I choose? 我父母希望我步入职业生涯，但是我应该选什么职业呢？

proficiency
 proficiency [prəˈfɪʃənsi] n. 熟练; 精通; His proficiency with guitar was obvious. 很明显，他十分精通吉他。

profile
 profile [ˈproʊˌfaɪl] n. 侧面像;  外形, 轮廓; vt. 描…的轮廓, 扼要描述; The picture shows the family members in profile. 这张图展现了家庭成员的侧面轮廓。

profit
 profit [ˈprɑfɪt] n.利润，益处 v.得益 The girl made a profit by selling the dress. 女孩卖掉了那些衣服，大赚了一笔。

progeny
 progeny [ˈprɑdʒəni] n.子孙，后代，成果 Our families want our progeny to be happy and successful when they grow up.

prognosis
 prognosis [prɑɡˈnoʊsɪs] n.[医] 预后；预知 We found the patient's cancer early, so his prognosis is good.

program
 program [ˈprəʊˌɡræm] n.节目单；大纲；程序 v.给...编写程序 My new tablet comes loaded with many different programs. 我的新平板电脑上有很多不同的程序。

progress
 progress ['prɑːɡres] n.进步；前进，进展 The chart showed that we were making progress, selling more every year. 图表说明随着销量一年高于一年，我们在进步。

progressive
 progressive [prəˈɡresɪv] adj. 前进的； 逐渐的； 渐进的； 发展的； 递增的； 累进的； Our business shows progressive growth for the last five years. 我们的生意在最近五年呈现出逐渐增长的形势。

prohibit
 prohibit [proʊˈhɪbɪt] v. 禁止 The law prohibits spitting in public. 该法令禁止在公共区域随意吐痰。

project
 project [prəˈdʒekt] n.计划，方案，工程 v.伸出，投影，规划 The housing project is going on well as planned. 这个建筑计划如期进展良好。

projectile
 projectile [prə'dʒɛktl] n.射弹 adj.发射的 When you run out of ammunition, humans can make for a good projectile. 当你弹尽粮绝的时候，人体炮弹也是一个不错的选择！

projection
 projection [prəˈdʒekʃ(ə)n] n.投射，投影 规划，预测 This projection of our future sales looks very healthy. 我们对未来销售的预测看起来很不错。

projector
 projector [prəˈdʒektər] n.放映机；投影仪 She showed him what a projector was. 珍妮向泰山展示了什么是投影仪。

 proliferate [prəˈlɪfəˌreɪt] v.激增，繁殖，增殖 Generation after generation, her descendants would proliferate. 一代又一代，她的后代不断增殖。

prolong
 prolong [proʊˈlɔŋ] v.延长，拉长，拖延 My teacher says he'll prolong the lesson by only one minute. 老师说他拖堂只拖一分钟（骗人）。

prominent
 prominent [ˈprɑmɪnənt] adj.突起的，凸出的；突出的，杰出的 The diamond is prominent among the stones. 钻石在鹅卵石中很突出。

promiscuous

promise
 promise [ˈprɑmɪs] n. 诺言;  有成功希望的预示;  允诺的事;  vi. 允诺;  有指望;  vt. 允诺, 保证; I promise that I am telling you the truth. 我保证我所言属实。

 promoter [prəˈmoʊtər] n.发起人；促进者 The promoter brought a billboard to advertise our product. 促销员拿来了一个广告牌来宣传我们的产品。

 pronghorn ['prɒŋ'hɔːn] n. 叉角羚; 糜鹿; You might find pronghorns roaming the plains. 你也许会看到有麋鹿在平原上漫步。

pronoun
 pronoun [ˈproʊˌnaʊn] n.代词 If you don't want to say a name, you can just use a pronoun like "he" or "him". 如果你不想说名字，你可以只用“他”这种代词。

proof
 proof [pruf] n.证据，证明，校样 v.校验 Have you had an affair? Don't deny it——I have proof! 你是不是有外遇了？别抵赖，我有证据！

propaganda
 propaganda [ˌprɑpəˈɡændə] n.宣传，宣传方法 They painted the slogans on the wall for propaganda. 为了宣传，他们把标语喷在了墙上。

propagation
 propagation [ˌprɒpə'ɡeɪʃn] n.繁殖；传播 Propagation of plants can be done from seed, or by taking cuttings and transplanting them. 植物繁殖可以通过播种，或者移植的方法实现。

 proper [ˈprɑpər] adj. 适用的, 适合的;  独特的;  真正的;  合乎体统的, 正派的, 正经的; adv. 完完全全地, 彻底地; "Which skirt is proper for a party?" she asked. “哪条裙子适合去晚会的时候穿？” 她问。

 properly [ˈprɑpərli] adv. 适当地; 正确地; 恰当地; If you go to a fancy dinner, you should dress properly. No T-shirts allowed! 如果你要去一场高贵晚宴，你应该穿着得当。不允许穿T恤！

property

proportional
 proportional [prə'pɔrʃənl] a.比例的；相称的 The amount of food served to them is proportional to their sizes. 给他们（爆破鬼才和虚空恐惧）上的食物跟他们的身材是成比例的。

proposal
 proposal [prəˈpoʊz(ə)l] n. 求婚; 建议; 提议; She made a romantic proposal to her boyfriend. 莫妮卡给了钱德勒一个浪漫的求婚。

   rightward : adj.在右的；向右的；右翼的|adv.在右地；向右地；右翼地
  
   right away : 立即，马上
  
  
 


rigid

 yellow [ˈjeloʊ] n.黄色 adj.黄色的 Look at this big yellow sunflower. 瞧这朵大的黄色向日葵。

yelp
 yelp [jelp] v.狗吠，(因痛而)叫喊，叫喊着说 She yelped in pain from the dog bite on her buttocks. 她屁股被狗咬了，她忍痛大喊起来。

yesterday
 yesterday [ˈjɛstədeɪ] n.昨天，往昔 adv.昨天 Today is Saturday, so Friday was yesterday. 今天是周六，所以昨天就是周五。

yet
 yet [jet] adv. 尚，还，仍然 I'm tired, but I haven't finished studying yet. 我很累，但还没学完。

yield
 yield [jild] v.出产，承认，屈服 n.产量，收益 The fields yielded many carrots for harvest this year. 这块田今年产出了很多胡萝卜。

yoga
 yoga ['joɡə] n.瑜珈, 瑜珈术 Penny got Sheldon to stretch his body in yoga. 佩妮带着谢耳朵舒展身体做瑜伽。

yogurt
 yogurt [ˈjoʊɡərt] n.(=yoghurt) 酸奶酪，酵母乳 Yogurt is a nice, light, nutritious snack. 酸奶是一种很好吃、清淡又营养的小吃。

yoke
 yoke [joʊk] n.牛轭；枷锁；纽带 v.结合，连结 The two oxen are attached together by a yoke over their necks. 脖子上的枷锁将这两头牛连在了一起。

yokel
 yokel [ˈjoʊk(ə)l] n.乡巴佬；庄稼汉 Some might call me a yokel - I don't care, I love my simple country life.

yolk
 yolk [joʊk] n.蛋黄 The recipe says that I should separate the yolk from the egg white. 食谱配方上标明，应将蛋黄和蛋清分离。

young
 young [jʌŋ] adj.年轻的，年纪小的；没有经验的 ；尚早的； 初期的 n.(动物的)崽；仔 The young cat is having fun with itself. 这只小猫正在自娱自乐。

youngster
 youngster [ˈjʌŋstər] n.年轻人 All the youngsters in my house listen to loud music. 我家里所有的孩子都爱听嘈杂的音乐。

yours
 yours [jɔrz] pron.你的，你们的（所属物） This car is yours now--drive safe! 这辆车现在是你的了，安全驾驶！

yourself
 yourself [jɔrˈself] pron. 你自己 You can do the painting by yourself. 你可以自己刷墙。

yourselves
 yourselves [jə'selvz] pron. 你们自己；你们本人（yourself的复数） Help yourselves to some food. 大家随便吃。

youth
 youth [juθ] n.青春；青年们；青年 I don't like the music the youth listen to these days. 我不喜欢现在这些青年人听的音乐。

youthful
 youthful [ˈjuθf(ə)l] adj. 年轻的;  富于青春活力的; That girl is so lovely and youthful. I like her! 那姑娘年轻又可爱。我好喜欢她！

yummy
 yummy ['jʌmi] n.美味 Wow, your head tastes great. It's positively yummy. 哇哦~你的脑袋尝起来不错！绝对的美味！

zeal
 zeal [zil] n.热心，热情 Rock Lee is full of zeal and vigor. 李洛克对所有事情都充满热情。

zenith
 zenith [ˈzenɪθ] n.顶点，顶峰；全盛 It was midday, and the sun was at its zenith. 正午时分，太阳到达了顶点。

zephyr
 zephyr [ˈzefər] n.和风，西风 A mild zephyr blows the seeds off the flower.

zero
 zero [ˈziroʊ] n.零，零度 num.零 I have had zero problems. 我没有问题。

zest
 zest [zest] n.兴趣，乐趣；滋味，风味 v.给…调味 His use of props added zest to an already interesting performance. 他使用的小道具给本来就有趣的表演又增添了乐趣。

zesty
 zesty ['zesti] adj. 刺激的，开胃的 A zesty lemonade drink is very refreshing when it's hot.

zigzag
 zigzag [ˈzɪɡˌzæɡ] n.之字形，折线 v.以之字形运动的 adj.曲折的，之字形的 adv.曲折地；之字形地；Z字形地 The paint left a zigzag mark on my shirt. 油漆在我的衬衫上留下了Z字形的记号。

zinc
 zinc [zɪŋk] n. 锌;  vt. 镀锌于…; Zinc is a very strong metal. 锌是一种非常强烈的金属。

zip
 zip [zɪp] v.拉拉链，飕飕飞过，注入活力 n.拉链，活力，飞射声 I make sure to zip up my pocket to keep my money safe. 我拉上口袋拉链以确保我的钱安全。

zipper
 zipper [ˈzipə(r)] vt. 用拉链扣住;  vi. 拉上拉链; n. 拉链 ; The red zipper is broken. 红色的拉链坏掉了。

zone
 zone [zoʊn] n.地区，区域，范围 Our school is in this zone. 我们学校在这个区。

zoo
 zoo [zu] n.动物园 There are so many animals in the zoo. 动物园里有好多动物。

zoology
 zoology [zuˈɑlədʒi] n.动物学；动物区系 The zoology of this part of Africa is endlessly interesting. 动物学在非洲这一板块有无限乐趣。

zoom
 zoom [zum] v.放大；急速上升，(价格)猛增 n.急速上升，图象电子放大，缩放；嗡嗡声 Let's zoom in to have a closer look. 让我们放大仔细看。

﻿abandon
 abandon [əˈbændən] v.抛弃；放弃 The mother has abandoned her baby. 这个母亲抛弃了她的孩子。
